  <script language="JavaScript">
   function getUrlParam(paramName)
{
                paramName = paramName.toLowerCase();
                var strReturn = "";
                var strHref = window.location.href;
                strHref = strHref.toLowerCase();
                var strQueryString = strHref.substr(strHref.indexOf("?"));
                if(strQueryString.indexOf(paramName + "=") &gt; -1 ) {
                                                                var aParam = strQueryString.split(paramName+"=");
                                                                if(aParam[1].indexOf("&amp;") &gt; -1)
                                                                {
                                                                                                var allParameters = aParam[1].split("&amp;")
                                                                                                strReturn = allParameters[0];
                                                                }
                                                                else
                                                                {
                                                                                                strReturn = aParam[1];
                                                                }
                                }
                                return strReturn;
}
function createCookie(name,value,days) {
	if (days) {
		var date = new Date();
		date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
		var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	}
	else var expires = "";
	document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}

function readCookie(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
}

tmo_data1 = {
	views : {
		xnt : {
			'ROS' : 5
		}
	}
}
tmo_util1 = {}
tmo_util1.readCookie = function (name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for (var i = 0; i &lt; ca.length; i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
			c = c.substring(1, c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
			return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
	}
	return null;
}
tmo_util1.getCookie1 = function (name, index_x) {
	var s = "xnt";
	var vd = tmo_data1.views;
	index_y = "";
	for (var i in vd[s])
		index_y = index_y + i + ";";
	ca = index_y.split(';');
	cunt_i = 0;
	for (var i = 0; i &lt; ca.length; i++) {
		if (ca[i] == name)
			break;
		cunt_i = cunt_i + 1;
	}
	mcookie = tmo_util1.readCookie(index_x);
	return mcookie.substring(cunt_i, cunt_i + 1);
}
tmo_util1.setViewCookies = function () {
	var c = "ROS";
	var s = "xnt";
	var dcuni
	var vd = tmo_data1.views;
	var index_x = "tmc" + s;
	var sync = tmo_util1.readCookie("dcsync" + s);
	var Lcoockie = tmo_util1.readCookie(index_x);
	if (!sync || !Lcoockie) { // create view cookies for all channels in site
		var str = 'view0'
	} else {
		var view = tmo_util1.getCookie1(c, index_x);
		if (view != null) {
			var t = vd[s][c];
			if (t) {
				view = (view % t) + 1;
				var str = '';
				str = 'view' + view
					dcuni = str;
			}
		} else {
			view = 0;
		}
	}
	return dcuni
}

		function  scrollToTkb (tkbId) {
		  if (tkbId &gt; 0) {
			 var xpos = 0;
			 var ypos =  xq('#tkb-' + tkbId).offset().top;
			 window.scrollTo(xpos,ypos);
			}

		}
		function scrollToReply(tkbId) {
			var xpos = 0;
			var ypos =  xq('#tkb-rep-' + tkbId).offset().top-50;
			x.talkbacks.showTb(tkbId)
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + tkbId + ' .reply-link a').click();
			window.scrollTo(xpos,ypos);		
		}		
		function getProfileImage() {
			var html = '';
			var src = '/images/blank1.gif'
    	
      var src = ''		 
			if (x.user.userpic_v1 != '' &amp;&amp; x.user.facebook_id == 0) {
				tmp = x.user.userpic_v1
        if (xq(tmp).attr('src') != '/images/blank1.gif') {
          src =  xq(tmp).attr('src')
        }		
			} else if (x.user.facebook_id != 0) {
				src = x.user.fb_pic_path		
			}
			
			var gender = '' 
			if (x.user.is_female == 1) {
				 gender = 'female';
			} else if (x.user.is_female == 0) {
				 gender = 'male';	
			} else if (x.user.is_female== 2) {
				gender = '';   
			}			
			
      			
			html = '&lt;div class="float"&gt;&lt;img class="v1 profile-image profile  ' + gender + '" src="' + src + '"/&gt;'
			if (x.user.facebook_id != 0){
				 html += '&lt;div class="fb-icon-wrap"&gt;&lt;div class="icon facebook v1"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'
			}
			html += '&lt;/div&gt;'
			return html;
		}

		function disableVoted() {
			xq('#tkb-msgs  .tkb').each(function (i) {
				var _id = xq(this).attr('tkbid');
				if(getCookie('Tb'+_id) == 1) {
					xq(this).find('.icon.thumbup, .icon.thumbdown').addClass('disabled');
				}
			});
		}
		
		function reloadTree () {
			xq('#tkb-pager .before').html('');
			xq('#tkb-pager .next').html('');
			xq('#tkb-msgs').html('')	
			var _url = '/Common/App/Talkbacks/CmmTalkbacksAJAX/0,14607,L-3107225_68_@o@_@p@_@pop@_@t@_@c@,00.html'
			if (1==2) {
				_url = '/Common/App/Talkbacks/CmmTalkbacksAJAX/0,14607,L-3107225_68,00.html'
			} else {
				_url = _url.replace(/@o@/,order);
				_url = _url.replace(/@p@/,page);
				_url = _url.replace(/@pop@/,popular);
				_url = _url.replace(/@t@/,talkbackType);
				_url = _url.replace(/@c@/,withContent);  		
			}
			
			var theDate = new Date();
			_url += '?t='+theDate.getTime();
			xq('#tkb-msgs').removeClass('withCont');
			xq.ajax({
				url: _url,
				success: function(data) {

					xq('#tkb-msgs').html(data);          			
				  if(withContent == 1) {
            xq('#tkb-msgs').addClass('withCont');
            //var _id = xq('.ad.hdn:first').attr('id');
			
				if(typeof tmo_api != 'undefined'){
					tmo_api.adRequest('ads.talkbacks_first.1', [300, 100], tmo_style.Talkback);
				}
			
          } 
					openDefaultTalkback();	
				}
			});					
		}	
		function openDefaultTalkback() {
			if (x._GET['tkb'] != null) {
				showTb(x._GET['tkb']);
				scrollToTkb(x._GET['tkb']);
			} 
			if (x._GET['tip'] != null) {
			    scrollToReply(0);
			    xq('.tkb-wrap .tab2').click();
			}
			if (x._GET['reply'] != null) {
			    scrollToReply(x._GET['reply']);
			}		      		
		}

		function setCookie(name, value, path, expires , domain, secure) {
			var curCookie = name + '=' + escape(value) + ((expires) ? '; expires=' + expires.toGMTString() : '') +
                 ((path) ? '; path=' + path : '') + ((domain) ? '; domain=' + domain : '') + ((secure) ? '; secure' : '');document.cookie = curCookie;
    	}
		function getCookie(c_name)
		{
	
		if (document.cookie.length&gt;0)
		  {
		  var c_start=document.cookie.indexOf(c_name + '=');
		  if (c_start!=-1)
		    {
		    c_start=c_start + c_name.length+1;
		    var c_end=document.cookie.indexOf(';',c_start);
		    if (c_end==-1) c_end=document.cookie.length;
		    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start,c_end));
		    }
		  }
		return '';
		}

	xq('.icon.thumbdown,.icon.thumbup').live('click', function() {
		var _parent = xq(this).parent();
		var action = 1;
		if(xq(this).hasClass('thumbdown')) {
			action = 2;
		} 

		
		var _rating = xq(_parent).find('.rat-val').html()
		if (_rating == '') {_rating = 0;}
		var _tkbId = xq(_parent).find('input[name=tkbId]').val()
		if(getCookie('Tb'+_tkbId) == 1) {
			return false;
		}
		xq(this).parent().find('.icon').addClass('disabled');
		var _url = '/Ext/App/TalkBack/CdaAddTalkbackRecommendation/1,11380,L-toReplace-contId-action,00.html'
		_url = _url.replace('toReplace',_tkbId);
		_url = _url.replace('contId',contId);
		_url = _url.replace('action',action);
		
		var _nrating  = action == 1 ? parseInt(_rating)+1 : parseInt(_rating)-1;
		
		if (_nrating &gt; 0) {
			xq(_parent).find('.sign').html('+')
		} else {
		    xq(_parent).find('.sign').html('')
		}
		xq(_parent).find('.rat-val').html(_nrating)
		 		
		xq.ajax({
			url: _url,
			success: function(data) {
				 setCookie('Tb'+_tkbId, '1', '/');
			}
		});	        
		return false;
	   
	     
	});

		function selectTab (className) {
			xq('.tkb-wrap .colorTitle span').each(function () {
				if (xq(this).hasClass(className)) {
					xq(this).removeClass('x999999')
					xq(this).addClass(colorChannel)					
				} else {
				   xq(this).removeClass(colorChannel)
				   xq(this).addClass('x999999')
				}
			});	
		}

	function afterInsert(e,place_pid,is_fb_publish) {
		if (e) {
			alert(' :' + e);
		} else if (is_fb_publish == 1){
		var _url = '/Common/Api/Facebook/CdaFacebookPublish/1,14719,@id@,00.html'  
  		_url = _url.replace(/@id@/,contId);
  		var theDate = new Date();
  		_url += '?t='+theDate.getTime();
  		xq('#fbPublishFrame').attr('src',_url)
		}
		
		inProgress = 0;

		xq('#tkb-rep-' + place_pid + ' .TabContent').html(xq('#tkb-thanks').html());		
		if (typeof(window.pageRefreshEnable)=='function') { window.pageRefreshEnable(); }
		isRefreshLock = 0;
	}
	
	var obj_child_count = new Array();
	
	function showTb(tkb_id,force_show) {
		
		// identifying a child's clicking
		var obj_child = xq('#tkb-' + tkb_id).find('.tkb.child');
		var parent_id = xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).parents().filter('.thread').find('.tkb.root').attr('tkbid');
		
		if(!obj_child_count[parent_id]){
			obj_child_count[parent_id] = 0;
		}
		
		if (xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).html() != '') {
			if(force_show == 1) {
				xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).show();
				xq('[name=tkbads_'+tkb_id+']').show();
				Url = window.location.pathname;
				ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Talkback_open', Url, dcPath, 2);
			
			} else {
				if(xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).css('display') == 'none') {
					xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).show();
					xq('[name=tkbads_'+tkb_id+']').show();
					Url = window.location.pathname;
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Talkback_open', Url, dcPath, 2);
		
				} else {
					xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).hide();
					xq('[name=tkbads_'+tkb_id+']').hide();
				}
				
				if(obj_child.length &gt; 0){
					if(xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).css('display') == 'none'){
						obj_child_count[parent_id]++;
					} else {
						obj_child_count[parent_id]--;
					}
				}
			}
			
			if(xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).css('display') == 'none') {
				xq('[name=tkbads_'+tkb_id+']').hide();
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + tkb_id).hide();
			} else {
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + tkb_id).show();
			} 
		} else {
			
			url = '/Common/App/Talkbacks/CmmShowTalkback/0,14604,L-@contId@_@type@_@tid@,00.html'
			url = url.replace(/@tid@/,tkb_id);
			url = url.replace(/@contId@/,contId);
			url = url.replace(/@type@/,conType);	
 			var theDate = new Date();
			url += '?t='+theDate.getTime();			
			xq.ajax({
				url: url,
				success: function(data) {
					data = xq(data);
					if(getCookie('Tb'+tkb_id) == 1) {
						data.find('.icon.thumbup, .icon.thumbdown').addClass('disabled');
					}					
					data.find('.open img').click(function() {

					});
                   
					if(obj_child.length &gt; 0){
						obj_child_count[parent_id]--;
						xq('[name=tkbads_par_'+parent_id+']').show();
						
							if(typeof tmo_api != 'undefined'){
								tmo_api.adRequest('ads.talkbacks_par.'+parent_id, [300, 100], tmo_style.Talkback);
							}
						
					}
				
					xq('[name=tkbads_'+tkb_id+']').show();
					
					// ads
					
						if(typeof tmo_api != 'undefined'){
							tmo_api.adRequest('ads.talkbacks.'+tkb_id, [300, 100], tmo_style.Talkback);
						}
					
					xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).html('').append(data).show();                               
					//xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).html(data).show();	
				}
			});	
			Url = window.location.pathname;
			ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Talkback_open', Url, dcPath, 2);
		} 
		
		if(obj_child_count[parent_id] &lt; 0){
			xq('[name=tkbads_par_'+parent_id+']').show();
		} else {
			xq('[name=tkbads_par_'+parent_id+']').hide();
		}
		
		
	}

	function openImgBind(tkb_id,is_prev) {
		var _html = xq('.tkb-bigImage').clone(true)						
		xq(_html).find('.body .img').html('&lt;img src="'+xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).find('input[name=image_path]').val()+'"/&gt;');
		xq(_html).find('.body .img-desc').html(xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).find('.desc').html())
		xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).find('.imgBig-wrap').html(_html);
		xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).find('.imgBig-wrap .tkb-bigImage').show();
		xq(_html).find('a.close').click(function() {
			xq('#tkb-cont-' + tkb_id).find('.imgBig-wrap .tkb-bigImage').hide();
			return false;
		})	
	}


	function checkForm(pid) {
		var obj = xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid)

		if (xq(obj).find('.errorMsg').html().length &gt; 1) {
			return false;
		}
		
		if (xq(obj).find('input[name=username]').val() == '   ') {
			xq(obj).find('input[name=username]').addClass('error');
			return false;
		}
		if (xq(obj).find('input[name=title]').val() == '   ') {
			xq(obj).find('input[name=title]').addClass('error')
			return false;
		}		
		
		if (xq(obj).find('input[name=username]').val().length &lt; 1) {
			xq(obj).find('input[name=username]').addClass('error').val('   ')
			return false
		} 
		if (xq(obj).find('input[name=title]').val().length &lt; 1) {
			xq(obj).find('input[name=title]').addClass('error').val('   ')			
			return false
		} 
		if (xq(obj).find('input[name=title]').val().length &gt; 40) {
			alert('     40   ')
			return false	
		}
		return 1;	
	}
	
	/* save and preview*/
	function trans(pid,img_id,is_preview,is_preview_image,img_path,img_path_420w) {
		 
		if (img_path_420w != null &amp;&amp; img_path_420w != '') {
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=img_420w]').val(img_path_420w);
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=img_85x85]').val(img_path);		
		} 
		if (img_path  != undefined &amp;&amp; img_path != '') {
			// lets prev image
			var fpath = imgServer +  img_path
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .desc img.prev').attr('src',fpath)
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=uploadedImgId]').val(img_id)	
		}
		if (is_preview_image == 1) {
			return false;
		}
		
		if(!checkForm(pid)) {
			return false;
		}
		
		if(is_preview == 1) {
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=preview]').val(1)
			xq('.rep-form .preview-wrap .close').click(function() {
				xq('.rep-form .preview-wrap .body').html('');
				xq('.rep-form .preview-wrap').hide(); 
				return false;	
			});
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=img_420w]').val(img_path_420w);
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=img_85x85]').val(img_path);				 
		} else {
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=preview]').val(0)
		} 

         var theDate = new Date();
		xq('#tkb-submit-form').attr('action','/Common/App/Talkbacks/CmmTalkbacksTrans/1,14605,L-0,00.html?t='+theDate.getTime());
		inProgress = 1;
		
		if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=is_anonymous]').val() == 1) 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_anonymous]').val(1)
		else
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_anonymous]').val(0) 		

		if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=is_fb_publish]').val() == 1) 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_fb_publish]').val(1)
		else
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_fb_publish]').val(0) 

		if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=is_publish]').is(':checked')) 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_publish]').val(1)
		else
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_publish]').val(0)

			 			
		if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=publish]').val() == 'postback') 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_postback]').val(1)
		else
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_postback]').val(0) 



			
			
			
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_tip]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).data('is_tip'))
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=img_id]').val(img_id)
		
		/* pid of thread */

		var root_tid = xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=thread_tid]').val()

		if (root_tid &gt; 0) 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=pid]').val(root_tid)
		else 
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=pid]').val(pid)	
		
	 			
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=place_pid]').val(pid) 	
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=browser]').val(x.talkbacks.browser)		
		if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=img-desc]').val() != ' ') {
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=img_desc]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' textarea[name=img-desc]').val())
		} else {
			xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=img_desc]').val('')
		}
	
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=title]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=title]').val());
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=username]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=username]').val());

		
		xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .wysiwyg-reply').wysiwyg('toBB');                      
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=description]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .wysiwyg-reply').data('bbcode'));
		xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=description_text]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .wysiwyg-reply').find('.xwysiwyg_content').text());
		//xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=description]').val(xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .wysiwyg-reply ').html())
		
		Url = window.location.pathname;
		
		if (xq('#tkb-submit-form input[name=is_tip]').val() == 1) {
			ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Tips_Send_Click', Url, dcPath, 2);
		} else {
			ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Talkback_Send_Click', Url, dcPath, 2);
		}

		xq('#tkb-submit-form').submit();
		return pid;
	}
	
	function validate_file(obj) {
		var _file =  xq(obj).val().toLowerCase();
		if(_file.lastIndexOf('.jpg')!=-1) 
        	return 1; 
		if(_file.lastIndexOf('.gif')!=-1) 
        	return 1;
		if(_file.lastIndexOf('.png')!=-1) 
        	return 1;
					
		return 0;   	
	}
	
	function setContId(_contId) {
		contId =_contId; 
	}                    
		
	/* t_tid = root thread talbkack id */	
	function showTbReply(pid,t_tid) {
		var preview = 0,
			preview_img = 0,
			img_id  = 0,
			is_tip  = 0,
        	inProgress = 0,
			newFileUpload = 0
			
    

    var openAfterSubmit = false;
    if (xq('#tkb-' + pid).find('.reply-link a').html() ==  ' ' &amp;&amp; xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('input[name=username]').length ==0 &amp;&amp; xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('.thanks').length !=0) {
        openAfterSubmit = true;
    }
    
    if (pid!= 0 &amp;&amp; openAfterSubmit != true &amp;&amp; (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).html() != '')) {
      xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).toggle();
			if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).css('display') == 'block') {
				xq('#tkb-' + pid).find('.reply-link a').html('  ');					
			} else {		
				xq('#tkb-' + pid).find('.reply-link a').html(' ');	
			}			
		} else {  
		  xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).show();       
		  if(pid != 0)
		    xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('.rep-form').remove();
		  else
		    xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('.rep-form .rep-form').remove();  
			var html = xq('#rep-form-hdn').clone(true);
			html.children('form').attr('id', 'tkb-rep-' + pid);		

			if (t_tid == undefined) 
				t_tid = pid
				
			var profile = getProfileImage()
			html.find('.userPic').html(profile);  	
			
	        html.find('.rep-form input[name=thread_tid]').val(t_tid)      
		    
		    html.find('.wysiwyg-reply').wysiwyg();
		    
		    html.find('.user_connect .register').get(0).href =  html.find('.user_connect .register').get(0).href.replace('@tkb@',pid);
		    html.find('.user_connect .login').get(0).href =  html.find('.user_connect .login').get(0).href.replace('@tkb@',pid);
		    
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .wysiwyg-reply').attr('id','wysiwyg-reply-' + pid);
			
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).data('is_tip',0)
			
					
			if (x.user.uid == 0) {
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).addClass('frmAnonymous');            
				html.find('input[name=publish]:eq(1)').attr('disabled', true);
			} else if (x.user.facebook_id != 0) {			                               
				html.find('input[name=username]').val(x.user.fullname)
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).addClass('frmFacebook');
			} else {
				html.find('input[name=username]').val(x.user.fullname)
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).addClass('frmLoggedIn');
			}
			
			 
			html.find('.wysiwyg-reply').attr('id','wysiwyg-reply-' + pid)	
		    html.find('.rep-form .prevBtn, .rep-form .submit-btn').click(function() {
		    	preview  = xq(this).is('.submit-btn') ? 0 : 1; 
		    	var _frm = xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' form').get(0)
		    	  
		    	var _url = 'http://upl.xnet.co.il/cgi/talkbacks_upload.asp';
		    	_url = _url + '?pid=' + pid + '&amp;is_preview=' + preview 
				if(newFileUpload) {
			    	xq(_frm).attr('action',_url);  	    	
					xq(_frm).submit();					
				} else {
					var _tmp_img_id = xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=uploadedImgId]').val();
					var _image_path =  xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('input[name=img_85x85]').val();
					var _image_path_420w =  xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('input[name=img_420w]').val();		
					trans(pid,_tmp_img_id,preview,'',_image_path,_image_path_420w)
				}
		  	
		    });
			   
            html.find('.regularRadio').mouseover(function() {
				xq(this).find('.help').html(xq('.tkb-formHelp-wrap').html()).show();
				xq(this).find('.help .body').html('  .   xnet    ')											
			});
            html.find('.regularRadio').mouseout(function() {
              xq(this).find('.help').html('').hide();		
			});
			
            html.find('.postbackRadio').mouseover(function() {
				xq(this).find('.help').html(xq('.tkb-formHelp-wrap').html()).show()
				xq(this).find('.help .body').html('  .      ')											
			});
            html.find('.postbackRadio').mouseout(function() {
                xq(this).find('.help').html('').hide();		
			});
			
			html.find('.radioGrp').each(function() {
				var radioGrp = xq(this),
					defaultValue = 'regular'
			
				if( defaultValue != '' ) {
					var vars = radioGrp.find('var');
					for(var i = 0; i &lt; vars.length; i++)
						if(xq(vars.get(i)).text() == defaultValue)
							xq(vars.get(i)).parent().parent().addClass('checked');
				}	
				
				radioGrp.find('.radio').each(function(index) {
					if (x.user.uid != 0) {
						xq(this).click(function() {
							radioGrp.find('.radio.checked').removeClass('checked');
							xq(this).addClass('checked');
							radioGrp.find('input').val( radioGrp.find('var:eq(' + index + ')').text() );						
						});					
					}
				});
			});
	    
	      
			html.find('.checkGrp').each(function() {
				var checkGrp = xq(this),
					cloneInput = xq('&lt;input type="hidden"/&gt;');
				
				checkGrp.find('p').each(function(index) {
					xq(this).click(function() {
						var p = xq(this).toggleClass('checked');
						var _name = xq(this).find('var').attr('name')
						if(_name == 'is_anonymous') {
							if(p.hasClass('checked')) {
								xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('[name=username]').attr('readonly',true)
							} else {
								xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).find('[name=username]').removeAttr('readonly')
							}  
						}
						if(p.hasClass('checked')) {
							var pVar = p.find('var');
							cloneInput.clone().appendTo(pVar).attr('name', pVar.attr('name')).attr('value', pVar.text());
							}
							else p.find('var input').remove();
					});
				});
			});
				
			if (x.user.uid == 0) {
			  html.find('.checkGrp').hide();
			  html.find('.postbackRadio var').css('background-position','-90px -41px')
			  html.find('.postbackRadio').addClass('disabled')		  
			} else if (x.user.facebook_id == 0) {
			  html.find('.checkGrp').eq(1).hide();
			}	 	
	
		   
		    html.find('input').focus(function () {
				if(xq(this).hasClass('error')) {
					xq(this).val('');
					xq(this).removeClass('error');					
				}						
			})
			
		    if (pid != 0) {
				html.find('.rep-form .close_btn').hide();
			} 
		    html.find('.rep-form .close_btn').click(function() {
		      if (pid == 0) {
			  	xq('#tkb-rep-0 .form-wrap').hide();
			  	xq('#tkb-rep-0 .empty').show();
			  } 
		    })
		    
             html.find('.rep-form input[name=file_1]').change(function() {
			 	xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .errorMsg').html('');         	
             	if(validate_file(this)) {
             		xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .desc img.prev').attr('src','/images/tkb_upload_cam.jpg')
					 newFileUpload = 1				 
				} else {
					xq('.img-wrap .errorMsg').html('    : jpg, gif, png')
				}

             })
             
            // ie7
		    html.find('input:file').keypress(function() {
		      return false;
		    });     
			 html.find('.rep-form .load-img-btn').click(function() {
			 	if(newFileUpload == 1) {
			    	preview_img  = 1;
			    	newFileUpload = 0; 
			    	var _frm = xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' form').get(0)
					  
			    	var _url = 'http://upl.xnet.co.il/cgi/talkbacks_upload.asp';
			    	_url = _url + '?pid=' + pid + '&amp;action=' + 'prevImage'
			    	xq(_frm).attr('action',_url);  	    	
					xq(_frm).submit();					 	
				 }
			 })
				

			xq('.tkb-wrap .tab').click(function () {
        if (xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid) &amp;&amp; xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' input[name=username]').length == 0) {
          xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .main-tkb-form .rep-form').remove();
          showTbReply(0,0);
        }	
			  
				if(xq(this).hasClass('tab1')) {	
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).data('is_tip',0)                                                
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).removeClass('tip'); 
					xq('.tkb-wrap .tab2').removeClass('active')
					xq('.tkb-wrap .tab2').addClass('inactive')
					xq('.tkb-wrap .tab1').addClass('active')
					xq('.tkb-wrap .tab1').removeClass('inactive')					
					xq('.tkb-wrap .content_1').show();
					xq('.tkb-wrap .content_2').hide();
					xq('#tkbc_anon_label').html('  (   )');
					xq('.tkb-wrap .publishWrap').show();
			  		xq('.tkb-wrap .form-wrap').show();
			  		xq('.tkb-wrap .empty').hide();					
				} else {
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).data('is_tip',1) 
				//xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).addClass('tip');
					
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .tab2').addClass('active')
						xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .tab2').removeClass('inactive')
					
						xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .tab1').removeClass('active')
						xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .tab1').addClass('inactive')
					
			  		xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .form-wrap').show();
			  		xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .empty').hide();					
					
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .content_1').hide();
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .content_2').show();
					xq('#tkbc_anon_label').html('  (   )');
					xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid +  ' .publishWrap').hide(); 
				} 	
			});
			if (pid == 0)
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .main-tkb-form').append(html.children());
			else 
				xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid).append(html.children());	
			xq('#tkb-' + pid).find('.reply-link a').html('  ');					
		}
			
	}	
	
	function setTextboxDefault (field,is_set,defaultTxt) {
		if (is_set == 1) {
			if(field.value=='')
				field.value=defaultTxt;		
		} else {
			if(field.value==defaultTxt)
				field.value='';
		}
	}


	function setUploadError(err,pid) {
		if(err == 'FileTooBig') {
			xq('#tkb-rep-' + pid + ' .errorMsg').html('       800K') 
		}
	}
	function toPage(p) {
		setPage(p);
		
		reloadTree();			
	}
  	
	return {
		postDisabled: postDisabled,	
		trans: trans,
		showTbReply: showTbReply,
		browser: browser,
		afterInsert: afterInsert,
		showTb: showTb,
		setTextboxDefault: setTextboxDefault,
		setContId: setContId,
		setUploadError: setUploadError,
		colorChannel: colorChannel,
		toPage: toPage,
		disableVoted: disableVoted,
		scrollToReply: scrollToReply,
		openImgBind: openImgBind,
		previewShow: previewShow,
		closeThanks: closeThanks
	};
	
})();

						}, carousel_C104630.speed, 'linear', function(){	
							xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro, .rectangle, .rectangle2').html('');							
							
							xq('.TopStory.C104630 .container').append(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first')).css('left', 0);
							
							
							 if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro').html() == '') {						
								 xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro').html(metroIframe);
							 }
							 if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle').html() == '') {						
								 xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle').html(rectIframe);
							 }
							 if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle2').html() == '') {						
								 xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle2').html(rectIframe2);
							 }
							
							carousel_C104630.disableBtn = 0;
						});
					},
					next: function(){ // left btn
						if(carousel_C104630.disableBtn == 1)
							return false;
							
						//alert('la' + xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro').html());	
						carousel_C104630.disableBtn = 1;
						xq('.TopStory.C104630 .container').prepend(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:last')).css('left', -carousel_C104630.colWidth);
						xq('.TopStory.C104630 .container').animate({
						  left: '+=' + carousel_C104630.colWidth + 'px'
						}, carousel_C104630.speed, 'linear', function(){
							if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro').html() == '') {						
								xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.metro').html(metroIframe);
							}
							if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle').html() == '') {						
								xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle').html(rectIframe);
							}
							if(xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle2').html() == '') {						
								xq('.TopStory.C104630 li.Strip:first').find('.rectangle2').html(rectIframe2);
							}
							carousel_C104630.disableBtn = 0;
						});
					}
				};
				
				xq('.TopStory.C104630 .leftBtn').click(function(){
					carousel_C104630.next();					
				});
				
				xq('.TopStory.C104630 .rightBtn').click(function(){
					carousel_C104630.prev();
					
				});				
				
				if (xq('.TopStory.C104630 .Strip3col .container li.Strip').length &gt; 1) {
					xq('.TopStory.C104630 .Arrows').show();
				}
			
			var tsstrip=0;
			xq('.TopStory .Strips.C104630 .Strip3col li').each(function () {
				if (xq(this).outerHeight() &gt; tsstrip) {
					tsstrip = xq(this).outerHeight();
				}
			});
			xq('.TopStory .Strips.C104630 .Strip3col li').css({'height':tsstrip, 'width':'360px'});
			
				// 3-col strip arrows
				xq('.TopStory .Strips.C104630 .Arrows').click(function(){
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'TopStoryWide', 'TS_Order_Arrows_Footer', dcPath);
				});
				
				// 3-col strip items
				xq('.TopStory .Strips.C104630 .Strip3col .Strip .ContentLink').click(function(){
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'TopStoryWide', 'TS_Order_Link_Footer', dcPath);
				});
				
				// Middle picture arrows
				xq('.TopStory.C104630 .ListImages.C104630 .nextBtnStrips').click(function(){	
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'TopStoryWide', 'TS_Pics_Arrows_Footer', dcPath);
					if (typeof autoPicMove104630 != 'undefined') {	
						clearTimeout(autoPicMove104630);
						currImage_104630 ++;
						if (currImage_104630 == totalImages_104630) {
							currImage_104630 = 0;
						}							
						
						autoPicMove104630 = setTimeout(function () {
							if ( movePicsRight_104630 == 1) {
								xq('.TopStory.Wide .ListImages.C104630 .HiddenRight').click();
							}
						},mainPicTiming_104630[currImage_104630]);													
						movePicsRight_104630 = 1;
					}
				});	
				
				xq('.TopStory.C104630 .ListImages.C104630 .prevBtnStrips').click(function(){	
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'TopStoryWide', 'TS_Pics_Arrows_Footer', dcPath);
					if (typeof autoPicMove104630 != 'undefined') {				
						clearTimeout(autoPicMove104630);
						currImage_104630 --;
						if (currImage_104630 == -1) {
							currImage_104630 = totalImages_104630 - 1;
						}						
						
						autoPicMove104630 = setTimeout(function () {
							if (movePicsRight_104630 == 0) {
								xq('.TopStory.Wide .ListImages.C104630 .HiddenLeft').click();
							}
						},mainPicTiming_104630[currImage_104630]);													
						movePicsRight_104630 = 0;
					}
					
				});
				
				// Middle picture link
				xq('.TopStory.C104630 .ListImages.C104630 a').click(function(){
					ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'TopStoryWide', 'TS_Pics_Link_Footer', dcPath);
				});
			
			
			xq(window).scroll(function(){
					var topBtn = parseInt(xq(window).height()/2);
					var scrollTop = (xq(window).scrollTop());
					var containerLimit = xq('.TopStory.C104630').height();
					var topOffset = xq('.TopStory.C104630').offset().top;
					var btns = xq('.TopStory .ListImages.C104630 .prevBtnStrips, .TopStory .ListImages.C104630 .nextBtnStrips, .TopStory .Strips.C104630 .Arrows');							
					
					if ((topOffset-scrollTop+115) &lt; topBtn) {						
						newTopBtn = scrollTop + topBtn - topOffset;
						//console.log('here we go: ' + newTopBtn);						
					} else {
						newTopBtn = 115;
						//console.log('start!: ' + newTopBtn);
					}
					
					if (scrollTop+topBtn &gt; topOffset+containerLimit-163) {
						newTopBtn = containerLimit - 163;
						//console.log('stop!: ' + newTopBtn);
					}										

					btns.stop().animate({'top': newTopBtn + 'px'}, 300);					
				}); 		
		
		});
     </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    xq('.ShoppingStrip .Strip').live('click', function(){
                var link = xq(this).find('a').attr('href');
                window.location.href = link;
            });
            
            xq('.ShoppingStrip .BtnCarousel').live('click', function(){
            
                if(xq(this).hasClass('disable'))
                    return false;
                xq('.ShoppingStrip .Links .container').css('width','5000');        
                var b = xq(this);
                var base = xq(this).parent().find('.container');
                var item_height = xq(this).parent().find('.group').outerWidth();
                var items_per_group = 1;
                var total = parseInt(item_height * items_per_group);
                
                if(xq(this).hasClass('next')){
                    b.addClass('disable');
                    base.animate({
                        right: '-=' + total
                    }, 500, function() {
                        var e = base.find('.group:lt(' + items_per_group + ')');
                        base.append(e);
                        base.css('right', 0);
                        b.removeClass('disable');
                        
                        ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'XnetShoppingVCarouselArrow', 'NextArrow', dcPath);
                    });
                }

                if(xq(this).hasClass('prev')){
                    var e = base.find('.group').slice('-' + items_per_group);
                    base.css('right', -total);
                    base.prepend(e);
                    b.addClass('disable');
                    base.animate({
                        right: '+=' + total
                    }, 500, function() {
                        b.removeClass('disable');
                        
                        ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'XnetShoppingVCarouselArrow', 'PrevArrow', dcPath);
                    });

                }
                
            });

 jQuery.fn.FancyBox = function (options) {
     var viewportwidth;
     var viewportheight;
	 
	 if (typeof window.innerWidth != 'undefined')
     {
          viewportwidth = window.innerWidth,
          viewportheight = window.innerHeight
     }
	 
	 else if (typeof document.documentElement != 'undefined'
         &amp;&amp; typeof document.documentElement.clientWidth !=
         'undefined' &amp;&amp; document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0)
     {
           viewportwidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth,
           viewportheight = document.documentElement.clientHeight
     }
	  else
     {
           viewportwidth = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientWidth,
           viewportheight = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientHeight
     }
 jQuery('#facebookPromoterClose').live('click',function () {
        jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').remove();
        jQuery('#facebookPromotion').remove();
    });
    if(!jQuery('#facebookPromotion').is(':visible')) {
        
        jQuery('#facebookPromotion').height(jQuery( document ).height()+50)
        jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').css( 'top', viewportheight/2 - jQuery( '#facebookPromotiondata' ).height()/2);
        jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').css( 'left', parseInt( ( jQuery( document ).width() / 2 ) - jQuery( '#facebookPromotiondata' ).width()/2 ) );
        if (jQuery.browser.msie) {
            jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').css('position','absolute');
                jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').css( 'top', viewportheight/2 + jQuery(document).scrollTop()- jQuery( '#facebookPromotiondata' ).height()/2);
        }
        jQuery('#facebookPromotiondata').show();
        jQuery('#facebookPromotion').show();
    }
    return this;
    
};    

function createCookie(name,value,days) {
    if (days) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
        var expires = '; expires='+date.toGMTString();
    }
    else var expires = '';
    document.cookie = name+'='+value+expires+'; path=/';
}

function readCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = name + '=';
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
    return null;
}

			function getFlashVersion() {
				var replaceRegexp = new RegExp(String.fromCharCode(92)+'D+','g');
				var matchRegexp = new RegExp('^,?(.+),?' + String.fromCharCode(36));
				try {
					try {
						  var axo = new ActiveXObject('ShockwaveFlash.ShockwaveFlash.6');
						  try { axo.AllowScriptAccess = 'always'; }
						  catch(e) { return '6,0,0'; }
						} catch(e) {}
						return new ActiveXObject('ShockwaveFlash.ShockwaveFlash').GetVariable(String.fromCharCode(36) + 'version').replace(replaceRegexp, ',').match(matchRegexp)[1];
				} catch(e) {
					try {
						if(navigator.mimeTypes['application/x-shockwave-flash'].enabledPlugin){
							return (navigator.plugins['Shockwave Flash 2.0'] || navigator.plugins['Shockwave Flash']).description.replace(replaceRegexp, ',').match(matchRegexp)[1];
						}
					} catch(e) {}
				}
				return '0,0,0';
			}


			function hasFlash(){
			   var version = getFlashVersion().split(',').shift();
			   return version=='0';
			}

					var videoUrl = '';			
					if (url != undefined) {								
						videoUrl = url.split('/');								
						if (videoUrl.length &gt; 1) {
							var videoNameLength = videoUrl.length;
							videoUrl = videoUrl[videoNameLength-1];
						} else {
							videoUrl = url;
						}
					}							
					var videoString = '';
					if (xq('.media .view h3') != undefined &amp;&amp; xq('.media .view h3').html() != '') {
						videoString += xq('.media .view h3').html();
						videoString = videoString.replace(/'/g,'');								
					}
					if (videoUrl != '') {
						videoString += '[' + videoUrl + ']';
					}					

					return videoString;
							
				};

				/* Added Auto PlayList (25.10.12) */
				VideoPlayer.AutoPlayList = function(selectors){
					xq('#'+selectors.container).find('object').remove();
					if(clipIndex &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; playMainVideo == 0){
						clipIndex++;
						clipIndex = parseInt(clipIndex);
					}
					playMainVideo = 0;
					
					tStartArray = (clipIndex &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; playMainVideo == 0) ? clipIndex : tStartArray;
					setvideoId = (parentId != 0) ? parentId : setvideoId;
					
					if(typeof tMultiArray[setvideoId] == 'undefined'){
						this.goBack(selectors);
					}

					if(typeof tMultiArray[setvideoId] == 'undefined'){
						this.goBack(selectors);
						return false;
					}
					
					var nextvId = tMultiArray[setvideoId][tStartArray];

					if(xq('#' + nextvId).length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; disableAuto == 0 &amp;&amp; typeof nextvId != 'undefined'){
						parentId = setvideoId;
						xq('#' + nextvId).click();
						tStartArray++;
					} else {
						this.goBack(selectors);
					}
				};
				
				VideoPlayer.PostRollUpdate = function(selectors) {
					if(typeof tmo_api != 'undefined'){

						xq.ajax({
							url: 'http://ad.doubleclick.net/N6870/adx'+tmo_post+';sz=399x199;'+xnst_video+';tile=2;ord=' + (new Date()).getTime() + ';callback=?',
							timeout: 3000,
							dataType: 'json',
							success: function(data) {

								// when advertising does not exist in system
								if (data.AdUrl.length &lt; 1){
									//VideoPlayer.onFinish(selectors);
									return false;
								}
								
								// count playlist's videos
								resVideo = (count_video_playlist - 1);
								
								if(data &amp;&amp; data.AdUrl != ''){						
									//Change for task no.865 - remove linkUrl if an advertisment is not linked 
									if (!data.ClickUrl) {
										var tmpClickUrl = '';
									} else {
										var tmpClickUrl = escape(data.ClickUrl);
									}
								}
								
								// console.log($f());
								// console.log('data.AdUrl:' + data.AdUrl + ' tmpClickUrl:' + tmpClickUrl);
								
								$f().getClip(resVideo).update({
									url:		data.AdUrl,
									linkUrl:	tmpClickUrl
								});
							},
							error: function(){
								is_post_error = 1;
								//VideoPlayer.onFinish(selectors);
							}
						});
					}
				}
				
				VideoPlayer.onFinish = function(selectors) {
					if (typeof(window.pageRefreshEnable)=='function') { window.pageRefreshEnable(); }
					this.AutoPlayList(selectors);
				}
				
				VideoPlayer.onStart = function(clip, videoid) {
			
					if (typeof(window.pageRefreshDisable)=='function') { window.pageRefreshDisable(); }
					
				/* Removed Popularity JSP, 24.10.12 */
					// var url	 =	this.PopularityKey +
								// '?content=' + videoid +
								// '&amp;type=1' +
								// '&amp;time=' + Math.round(clip.fullDuration);
					// document.createElement('img').src = url;
				}
				
				VideoPlayer.goBack = function(selectors) 
				{
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('.gad').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('.clips').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).find('object').remove();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).find('.play').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).find('.stupidplay').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).find('.fakebar').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.content).hide();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('h3').removeClass('hdn');
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('em').removeClass('hdn');
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('div.none_opacity.top').removeClass('none_opacity top').addClass('opacity top');		
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().find('div.opacity.top').show();					
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('h3').html(xq('#'+selectors.container).find('.stupidityathisbest').html());
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('em').html(xq('#'+selectors.container).find('.credit').html());
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('h3, em').show();
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('.clips').find('div a').each(function(){
							xq(this).find('em').html(xq(this).find('img').attr('alt'));
						});
				}
				
		VideoPlayer.getVideoObject = function(vidurl, selectors, data, videoid, postdata) {
		
		
			/* Added fix bug OnMouseOver for title, (task 1124, 04.11.12)*/

				clearTimeout(timeout);
				showTitle();
			}).mouseleave(function(){
				timeout = setTimeout(function() {
					hideTitle();
				}, 500);
			});
					
			var GoogleAnalyticKey	= 'UA-21322368-3',
				FlowPlayerKey		= '#$82d88990cf33aa2235a',

			function stopVideo() {
		
				if (typeof(window.pageRefreshEnable)=='function') { window.pageRefreshEnable(); }
				VideoPlayer.goBack(selectors)
			}
			
			function showTitle() {
						xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('h3, em, div.opacity.top').show();}
			function hideTitle() {
				xq('#'+selectors.container).parent().children('h3, em, div.opacity.top').hide();}

				onPause: function (clip) {
					if (typeof(window.pageRefreshEnable)=='function') { window.pageRefreshEnable(); }
					var indexVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip().index;
					//var clipVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip(indexVideo).baseUrl;
					var clipVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip(indexVideo).originalUrl;
					var videoUrl = VideoPlayer.getVideoForGA(clipVideo);
					
					var timestamp = parseInt($f().clip = $f().getTime());
					if(clipVideo != undefined){
						ga('xnetTracker.send', 'event', 'Video_'+dcPath, 'Pause', videoUrl, timestamp);						
					}
				},
				onSeek: function (clip) {
					var indexVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip().index;
					//var clipVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip(indexVideo).baseUrl;
					var clipVideo = $f().clip = $f().getClip(indexVideo).originalUrl;

					}
				},

							S = xq(this).hasClass('left')?'+':'-';
						function hover() {
							var div = clips.find('div');
							if(S == '-' &amp;&amp; parseInt(div.css('left')) &lt; 1) return true;
							else if(S == '+' &amp;&amp; parseInt(div.css('left')) &gt; div.children('a').length * 143 -735) return true;
							else div.animate({left: S + '=10px'}, N);
						}
						hover();
						interval = setInterval(hover, N);
					}, function(){clearInterval(interval);});
				});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                    var d = new Date();
                    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
                    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
                    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + "; " + "path=/";
                }

                function getCookie(cname) {
                    var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for(var i=0; i&lt;ca.length; i++) {
                        var c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
                        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
                    }
                    return "";
                }
                
                function Validate() {
                    var emailFilter = /^.+@.+..{2,3}$/;
                    var txtMail = document.getElementById("mm_newemail_fa");
                    if (txtMail == null) {
                        alert('    .');
                        return false;
                    }
                    else if (!(emailFilter.test(txtMail.value))) {
                        txtMail.style.backgroundColor = "#ffcccc";
                        alert('   ');
                        txtMail.focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                    else {
                        txtMail.style.backgroundColor = "white";
                        setCookie('arch-design-popup', '1', 180);
                        
                        document.contentFormFashion.action = "https://webapi.mymarketing.co.il/Signup//PerformOptIn.aspx";
                        document.contentFormFashion.target = 'activeTrailIframe';
                        document.contentFormFashion.submit();
                        
                        // xq('.arch-design-popup').addClass('thanks');
                        xq('.arch-design-popup').css('background', 'url(/images/activeTrail/popup_thanks.jpg)');
                        xq('.arch-design-popup .fields').hide();
                        return true;
                    }
                }

        
                xq(document).ready(function(){
                    
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        if(getCookie('arch-design-popup') != 1 &amp;&amp; navigator.appVersion.indexOf('Mobile') == -1){
                            xq('.window, .arch-design-popup').show();
                        }
                    }, 10000);
                    
                    xq('.arch-design-popup .at-signup-input').focus(function(){
                        var v = xq(this).attr('place-holder');
                        if(v == 1){
                           xq(this).css('text-align', 'left'); 
                           xq(this).attr('place-holder', 0); 
                           xq('.arch-design-popup .at-signup-input').val(''); 
                        }
                    });
                    xq('.arch-design-popup .close').click(function(){
                        xq('.window, .arch-design-popup').hide();
                        setCookie('arch-design-popup', '1', 180);
                    });
                    xq('.arch-design-popup .fields .field.check').click(function(){
                        if(!xq(this).hasClass('v')){
                           xq(this).addClass('v');
                           xq(this).find('img').attr('src', '/images/fashion/cb_v.jpg');
                        } else {
                           xq(this).removeClass('v');
                           xq(this).find('img').attr('src', '/images/fashion/cb_empty.jpg');
                        }
                    });
                    xq('.arch-design-popup .btn').click(function(){
                        if(!xq('.arch-design-popup .fields .field.check').hasClass('v')){
                            alert('     ')
                            return false;
                        }
                        
                        Validate();
                    });
                });
   </script>
